 Remains in the court from ten to four in the morning
 iske baad ghar jaakar dedh ghante aaraam karte hai
 Then they start preparing for the next day's lawsuits
 har mukademe kii file dekhni hoti he
 a file is of 100 pages and some of fifty pages
 iske bich faisla bhi dictate karnaa hota he
 Go to sleep by half past eleven and wake up at five o'clock
 jajon ko tahalnaa acha lagata he
 After a walk from seven to eight in the morning, then prepare the case again
 saadhe nau baje ke aas paas court ke liye nikal jate hai
 Many judges also work late nights on Saturdays and Sundays
 mukademon ko daakhil karnaa, daakhil hue mukademon ko sunanaa, faisla likhane ke alaava unke anya prashasnic kaam bhi hote hai
 Their full potential is judged on how fast they listen to the case, understand it and pass judgment
 nichali adaalaton ke jajon kaa pramotion to inhen baton par tikaa hota he ki kitne cese ko niptaya he
 Can a judge read 50 files in a day
 subah saat baje se raat ke 11 baje tak jaj kaam karte hai, phir chuttee ke din bhi

 Those who are judges of constitutional bench are writing their decisions
 agar ek paksh taiyaar he to doosraa paksh taiyaar nahin he

 teen hafte kii chuttee hoti he

 sawaal he ki kya chuttee samaapt kar dene se jajon kii sankhya kii zarurat samaapt ho jaaegi

 aath hazaar ke kareeb jaj hai
 Can this deficiency be reduced by reducing the leave to three or four weeks
 kya ye mumkin hai ki koi jaj ek din main bees mukademon kii file dekh le
 He has to listen to both sides, read the law and write the decision
 bich-bich main shakespeare ko bhi kot karnaa hota he
 Now i understand why our judges continue to quote Shakespeare
 duusare kisi ko padhane kaa vakt hi nahin miltaa hoga
 The Supreme Court of America has 9 judges
 sabko milakar ek saal main 81 keson main faisla dena hota he
 In India, a judge hears an average of 2600 lawsuits, passing judgment
 chif justise ne kaha ki jab baahar se jaj aate hai to hamen dekhakar hairaan hote hai
 On 7 April, Pradeep Thakur wrote in the 'times of India' that according to a study, a High Court judge has only five or six minutes for a trial
 pehali baar aisa adhyayan hua he
 The busiest judge, that is, he who has a lot of cases, has only two and a half minutes to hear a case
 jo sabase kam vyast he uske paas maatr 15 se 16 minute hai
 They have to give a decision in five to six minutes
 bangaloru kii ek sanstha he daksh usne ye adhyayan kiya he
 For example, 163 judges come to the Kolkata High Court every day for a hearing
 ek cese ke liye do minute jitna hi samay hota he
 The judges of Patna, Hyderabad, Jharkhand, Rajasthan get two to three minutes for a case every day
 kya ek arab 25 karod kii aabaadi ke liye ucch or ucchtam nyaalayon ke 619 jaj paryaapt he
 The comments kisi ko bhi lagegaa ki uske saath koi mazaaq kar rahaa he
 Think who is joking with you
 aakhir sarkaron ne jajon kii sankhya kyon nahin badhaai
 Why did the facilities in the courts not be increased
 aapako insaaf se koun dur rakh rahaa he
 a man waits for forty years in the courts for a verdict
 uske faisle ke liye kisi jaj ke paas do minute kaa vakt nahin he
 His wait for decision is short
 tees chalis saal main jaj sahab kaa wo do minute mil jaae, uske liye hota he
 Will the solution come out of making a list of cases or is this question very easy by increasing the number of judges
 jawaab aap khud dijie
 The condition of Uttar Pradesh is worse
 pashchim uttar pradesh ke log kab se apane liye ek bench kii maang kar rahe hai
 Everything is sold from here on its way to Lucknow and Allahabad
 chif justise kii baat main yah bhi shaamil he ki adaalaton kii suvidhaon or dhaanchon par bhi dhyaan dena hoga
 a farmer in Meerut is saddened by how a lawsuit changed his life
 meerut se elahabaad hai court ke chakkar ne use barbaad kar diya he
 In 2008, 40 million cases were heard in Indian courts
 yah aankada duniya ke kisi bhi desh kii adaalat se kai guna zyada he

 justise balakrishnan ne kaha tha ki jajon kii itani kami he ki ek jaj ko ek cese par nazar daalane ke liye 25 minute se zyaada nahin milte

 builder ke paas bhi line

 sthaayee samiti ne suzav diya ki ise 10 se 50 kiya jaae

 is match main bhartiya varchasv kaa alam yah rahaa ki puri australian team ne match main 368 ran batore, jaaki bharat ke do ballobaajon-pujaara (204) or murali vijay (167) ne duusare wicket ke liye 370 ran jode the
 Now both teams will turn to Mohali, where the third Test match will be played at Punjab Cricket Association Ground (PCA) from 18 February
 chauthe din australia ke liye din kii shuruyaat aid kowan or shen watson ne kii

 bharat ko pehali pari ke aadhaar par 266 ranon kii badhat mili thi
 The work done by an astrologer and social worker here for water conservation can become an example for the whole country
 mandiron main dev pratimaaon ko arpit kiye jane vaale jal ke sangrakshan kaa anoothaa kaary yahaan kiya ja rahaa he
 Pandit Purushottam Gaur, popularly known as Guruji among his favorites, has developed water conservation structures in nearly 300 temples in Rajasthan in the last 13 years
 samaaj seva or jyotish ke kshetra main ullekhneey kaam karne ke liye goud ko maharana mewar award samet kai sammaanon se nawaja ja chukaa he
 In Hindu temples, millions of gallons of water offered by devotees flowed into the drains
 goud ne bataaya ki varsh 2000 main unhone apana jalabhishek abhiyaan shuru kiya
 41-year-old astrologer Gaud said, "I noticed that the water offered by the devotees in the temples goes completely waste in the drains
 isliye mujhe inkaa bhoojal ko richarge karne main istemaal karne kii yukti suujhi
 " iske baad unhone mandiron khaas kar shivalayon main jal sangrah karne kaa kaam shuru kiya
 The water is passed through several filter chambers before being sent to land
 goud ne kaha ki is pariyojna ke tahat mandiron main jan sahyog se kai tanks or borwell kaa nirmaan karaayaa gaya
 Gaud said, "in some temples, a 30-foot deep pit was required to be dug so that the water of the idols could be collected directly there
 pratimaaon par chadhaae jane vaale doodh ko jamaa karne ke liye paanch foot ke gadde kii alag se jarurat padi
 " goud ne aage kaha, "mujhe tab behad khushi hui jab kai vaigyanik or bhoojal visheshgy meri madad ke liye saamne aae or 'shiksha samiti' naam ke ek sanghathan ko is kaam main aage kiya
 The institute calculated that there are more than 300 temples in the city where at least 40 million liters of water is offered daily in the month of Shravan to the idols of Lord Shiva and other deities
 " unhone kaha ki is barbaadi ke alaava shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal or dugdh kaa paryaavaran par bhi vipareet prabhaav padataa he
 The comments goud ne bataaya, "aam taur par mandir ke sameep jal or dugdh ko nirbaadh bahane diya jaataa he
 This creates an unhealthy environment
 mandir ke chaaron ore machhar or mackhiyon ke palane kaa vaataavaran taiyaar ho jaataa he
 " jal sangrakshan ke kaam main pesh ai kathinaaiyon ke bare main goud ne bataaya ki shuru main iske liye pujaariyon ko manaa paanaa aasaan nahin tha
 He said that his efforts were viewed with suspicion by many priests
 yahaan tak ki jab unke samarthakon ne is pariyojna ke liye dhan jamaa karnaa shuru kiya tab bhi pujari anakani karte rahe
 But today 300 temples are associated with this campaign
 apane chaheton ke bich guruji ke naam se prasiddh pandit purushottam goud ne pichley 13 varsho main rajasthan ke kareeb 300 mandiron main jalsangrakshan dhaanche kaa vikaas kiya he
 Gaud has been awarded several honors including Maharana Mewar Award for his remarkable work in the field of social service and astrology
 hindu mandiron main bhakton dwaara arpit lakhon galen jal naaliyon main bah jaataa tha
 Gaud said that in the year 2000, he started his Jalabhishek campaign
 41 varshiya jyotishi goud ne bataaya, "maine gaur kiya ki mandiron main shraddhaluon dwaara arpit jal puri tarah naaliyon main bekaar chalaa jaataa he
 So i thought of using them to recharge ground water
 " After this, he started collecting water in temples, especially pagoda
 bhoomi main bhejne se pehle jal ko kai filter chambaron se guzaara jaataa he
 Gaur said that under this project many tanks and borewells were built in the temples with public support
 goud ne kaha, "kuch mandiron main 30 foot gaharaa gaddha khodne kii jarurat padi taaki pratimaaon kaa jal sidhaa vahaan ekatrit ho sake
 a separate five-foot pit was needed to deposit the milk to be mounted on the statues
 " Gaur continued, "I was very happy when many scientists and groundwater experts came to my aid and put forward an organization called 'shiksha Samiti' in this work
